      <title></title>
      <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/AppReportStandard.css" type="text/css"><script lanuage="javascript">
               /**
                * For the following languages, need to explicitly assign 
                * following specific fonts to ensure align:
                *
                *  Language    Font
                *  --------    --------
                *  ko          굴림체
                *  jp          ＭＳ ゴシック
                *  ch       新宋体
                *  tw       新宋体
                */
               function setFont()
               {
                  var mainWin;
                  if (window.opener != null) mainWin = window.opener.top;
                  else mainWin = window.top;
                  var lang =  "us" ;
                 	lang  = lang.toLowerCase();
                  var font = "";
                  if (lang == "ko")
                  {
                     font = "굴림체";
                  } 
                  else
                  if (lang == "jp")
                  {
                     font = "ＭＳ ゴシック";
                  }
                  else
                  if (lang == "ch" || lang == "tw")
                  {
                     font = "新宋体";
                  }
				
                  if (font.length > 0)
                     document.getElementsByTagName('pre')[0].style.fontFamily
                        = font;
               }
            </script></head>
